class="result-card__contents profile-result-card__contents"><h3 class="result-card__title profile-result-card__title">Anthony Heaphy</h3><h4 class="result-card__subtitle profile-result-card__subtitle">Co-Organizer at Data Science Ireland | AI and Data Science Recruiter | Helping Leaders connect with the Top talent in AI</h4><div class="result-card__meta profile-result-card__meta"><p class="profile-result-card__location"></p></div></div></li><div class="description__text description__text--rich"><p><strong>Senior Data Scientist</strong> </p><p><br> </p>Our client is a Global Tech company and is one of the top companies in the world in their sector,  who boasts one of the best Distribution engines for their product. The Data Science team drives the companies growth through innovative data science approaches to help distribute their product across millions of people worldwide.<p><br> </p><p>They are looking to build one of the top Data Science teams in Ireland and Europe and are looking for high-achieving Senior Data Scientists to join.&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;The Data Science team is Full stack where you will be tasked with managing the full cycle of the models from research to productionising and deploying of the models.&nbsp; </p><p><br> </p><p> <strong>What you will do</strong> </p><ul><li>Develop algorithms that deal with a variety of prediction tasks at scale </li><li>Build a user acquisition system, focusing on customer lifetime value through building incredibly dynamicand intelligent segmentation algorithms, predicting customers’ future spend on future products and optimizing bidding strategy.&nbsp;<br> </li><li>Play a key role in allocating budgets and revenue generation. Other areas you would be involved in are fraud detection and prediction of how various media streams will perform.<br> </li><li>Collaborate with non-technical managers, data engineers, and other data scientists to optimize the distribution of their products </li><li>Understand the business context of your work, conceptualize solutions, extract and prepare data, develop models, write production-ready code, deploy algorithms and track their performance. </li></ul><br><strong>Who you are</strong><br> <ul><li>Minimum of a Masters Degree in a Quant / Computer Science field -<strong><u>PhD bonus</u></strong> </li><li>3+ years of experience working as a data scientist or machine learning engineer on technically challenging problems </li><li>Studied at a Top univeristy and&nbsp;have demonstrated high achievement throughout your career </li><li>Experience with Time series analysis </li><li>Experience with Python or R as coding language of choice </li><li>Experience with Big Data tools&nbsp; </li><li>Knowledge of both Statistical data science techniques and engineering.  </li></ul><br><strong>Bonus</strong><br>Experience with real-time bidding algorithms <p><br> </p><p><strong>Benefits</strong> </p><ul><li>My client offers top market salary and benefit packages. </li><li>A clear progression structure for both future managers and individual contributors </li><li>Joining a company that has core values in People , Culture and Impact</li></ul></div><ul class="job-criteria__list"><li class="job-criteria__item"><h3
